The stage is set for the ultimate battle.</p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.4s; transition-delay: 0.255556s;"><strong><em>Time to pick a side</em></strong></p>
